This page provides consistent definitions for the core objects used across LI.FI’s API and SDK. Use these as the authoritative reference when building integrations.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#transfer-objects)

Transfer Objects
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#quote)

Quote

A **Quote** is a single-step transfer plan with transaction data ready for immediate execution. **Response from `GET /quote`:**

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Quote {
      id: string;                    // Unique quote identifier
      type: "lifi";                  // Quote type
      tool: string;                  // Bridge or DEX used (e.g., "stargate")
      action: Action;                // What happens in this transfer
      estimate: Estimate;            // Output amounts and fees
      transactionRequest: {          // Ready-to-sign transaction
        to: string;
        data: string;
        value: string;
        gasLimit: string;
        // ... other tx fields
      };
    }
    

**When to use:** Request a Quote via `/quote` when you want the best single route with transaction data included. Ideal for simple transfers.[Get Quote API\
-------------\
\
Request a quote for token transfers](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#route)

Route

A **Route** is a multi-step transfer plan that may require sequential transactions. **Response from `POST /advanced/routes`** (returns array of routes):

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Route {
      id: string;                    // Unique route identifier
      fromChainId: number;           // Source chain
      toChainId: number;             // Destination chain
      fromToken: Token;              // Source token
      toToken: Token;                // Destination token
      fromAmount: string;            // Input amount (wei)
      toAmount: string;              // Expected output (wei)
      steps: Step[];                 // Array of steps to execute
    }
    

**When to use:** Request Routes via `/advanced/routes` when you need multiple route options or want to compare alternatives. Each Step in a Route may require a separate transaction.[Get Routes API\
--------------\
\
Request multiple route options](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/get-a-set-of-routes-for-a-request-that-describes-a-transfer-of-tokens)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#step)

Step

A **Step** is one atomic operation within a Route. Each Step represents a single transaction. **Nested within Route response** (also returned by `POST /advanced/stepTransaction`):

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Step {
      id: string;                    // Unique step identifier
      type: "swap" | "cross" | "lifi" | "protocol";
      tool: string;                  // Bridge or DEX name
      toolDetails: ToolDetails;      // Logo, name, key
      action: Action;                // What this step does
      estimate: Estimate;            // Output estimates
      includedSteps?: Step[];        // Nested steps (for complex routes)
      transactionRequest?: {         // Transaction data (populated after stepTransaction call)
        to: string;
        data: string;
        value: string;
      };
    }
    

**Step types:**

*   `swap` - Same-chain token swap via DEX
*   `cross` - Cross-chain bridge transfer
*   `lifi` - Combined swap + bridge in one transaction
*   `protocol` - Interaction with a DeFi protocol (deposit, stake, etc.)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#action)

Action

An **Action** describes what happens in a Step - the source and destination tokens, chains, and amounts. **Nested within Quote/Step responses:**

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Action {
      fromChainId: number;           // Source chain ID
      toChainId: number;             // Destination chain ID
      fromToken: Token;              // Token being sent
      toToken: Token;                // Token being received
      fromAmount: string;            // Input amount (wei)
      slippage: number;              // Allowed slippage (e.g., 0.005 = 0.5%)
      fromAddress?: string;          // Sender address
      toAddress?: string;            // Recipient address (if different)
    }
    

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#reference-objects)

Reference Objects
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#tool)

Tool

A **Tool** is a bridge or exchange used to execute transfers. LI.FI aggregates 27 bridges and 31 exchanges. Use `GET /tools` for the current list. **Response from `GET /tools`:**

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Tool {
      key: string;                   // Unique identifier (e.g., "stargate")
      name: string;                  // Display name (e.g., "Stargate")
      logoURI: string;               // Tool logo URL
      supportedChains: Chain[];      // Chains this tool supports
    }
    

**Popular bridges:** `stargate`, `across`, `hop`, `cbridge` **Popular DEXs:** `1inch`, `paraswap`, `0x`, `uniswap`, `sushiswap`

Use `GET /tools` to get the current list of supported bridges and exchanges.

[List Tools API\
--------------\
\
Get all available bridges and exchanges](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-available-bridges-and-exchanges)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#chain)

Chain

A **Chain** represents a supported blockchain network. **Response from `GET /chains`:**

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Chain {
      id: number;                    // Chain ID (e.g., 1 for Ethereum)
      key: string;                   // Short key (e.g., "eth")
      name: string;                  // Display name (e.g., "Ethereum")
      chainType: "EVM" | "SVM" | "UTXO" | "MVM";
      coin: string;                  // Native token symbol
      logoURI: string;               // Chain logo URL
      metamask?: {                   // MetaMask connection info
        chainId: string;
        chainName: string;
        nativeCurrency: {...};
        rpcUrls: string[];
      };
    }
    

**Chain types:**

*   `EVM` - Ethereum Virtual Machine chains (Ethereum, Arbitrum, etc.)
*   `SVM` - Solana Virtual Machine
*   `UTXO` - Bitcoin and UTXO-based chains
*   `MVM` - Move Virtual Machine (SUI)

[List Chains API\
---------------\
\
Get all supported chains](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-information-about-all-currently-supported-chains)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#token)

Token

A **Token** represents a supported cryptocurrency on a specific chain. **Response from `GET /tokens`:**

Copy

Ask AI

    interface Token {
      address: string;               // Contract address (or native token identifier)
      chainId: number;               // Chain this token is on
      symbol: string;                // Token symbol (e.g., "USDC")
      name: string;                  // Full name (e.g., "USD Coin")
      decimals: number;              // Decimal places (e.g., 6 for USDC)
      logoURI?: string;              // Token logo URL
      priceUSD?: string;             // Current USD price
      coinKey?: string;              // Canonical token identifier across chains
    }
    

The same token (e.g., USDC) has different addresses on each chain. Use `coinKey` to identify the same asset across chains.

[List Tokens API\
---------------\
\
Get all supported tokens](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens)

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#status-objects)

Status Objects
------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#status)

Status

**Status** indicates the current state of a cross-chain transfer.

| Status | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `NOT_FOUND` | Transaction not yet indexed or invalid hash |
| `INVALID` | Transaction failed validation |
| `PENDING` | Transfer is in progress |
| `DONE` | Transfer completed (check substatus for details) |
| `FAILED` | Transfer failed (check substatus for reason) |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#substatus)

Substatus

**Substatus** provides detailed information within each Status.

#### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#pending-substatuses)

PENDING Substatuses

| Substatus | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `WAIT_SOURCE_CONFIRMATIONS` | Waiting for source chain confirmations |
| `WAIT_DESTINATION_TRANSACTION` | Bridge is processing, waiting for destination |
| `BRIDGE_NOT_AVAILABLE` | Bridge temporarily unavailable |
| `CHAIN_NOT_AVAILABLE` | Chain RPC issues |
| `REFUND_IN_PROGRESS` | Refund is being processed |
| `UNKNOWN_ERROR` | Temporary error, keep polling |

#### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#done-substatuses)

DONE Substatuses

| Substatus | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `COMPLETED` | Transfer successful, user received exact requested tokens |
| `PARTIAL` | Transfer successful, user received different token than requested |
| `REFUNDED` | Transfer failed but tokens were refunded to sender |

#### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#failed-substatuses)

FAILED Substatuses

| Substatus | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `NOT_PROCESSABLE_REFUND_NEEDED` | Cannot complete, manual refund required |
| `OUT_OF_GAS` | Transaction ran out of gas |
| `SLIPPAGE_EXCEEDED` | Received amount too low (price moved beyond allowed slippage) |
| `INSUFFICIENT_ALLOWANCE` | Token approval insufficient |
| `INSUFFICIENT_BALANCE` | Not enough tokens or gas |
| `EXPIRED` | Transaction expired |
| `UNKNOWN_ERROR` | Unknown or invalid state |
| `REFUNDED` | Tokens were refunded |

For the complete and authoritative status documentation, see the [Status Tracking Guide](https://docs.li.fi/introduction/user-flows-and-examples/status-tracking)
.

[Status Tracking Guide\
---------------------\
\
Complete guide to monitoring transfers](https://docs.li.fi/introduction/user-flows-and-examples/status-tracking)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#partial)

Partial

A transfer is **Partial** when it completes successfully but the user receives a different token than originally requested. **Why this happens:**

*   Destination chain swap failed after bridging
*   Insufficient liquidity for final swap
*   Price impact too high for destination swap

**What the user receives:**

*   The bridged token (e.g., USDC.e instead of native USDC)
*   Full value is preserved, just in a different token

**How to handle:**

1.  Check `substatus === "PARTIAL"` when `status === "DONE"`
2.  Read `receiving.token` from status response for actual received token
3.  Inform user they received equivalent value in different token

[Intermediate Tokens Guide\
-------------------------\
\
Understanding PARTIAL status and intermediate tokens](https://docs.li.fi/guides/intermediate-tokens)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#refunded)

Refunded

A transfer is **Refunded** when it fails but the user’s tokens are returned to their wallet. **When refunds happen:**

*   Bridge execution failed
*   Destination chain issues
*   Transfer expired

**Refund location:**

*   Usually returned to sender on the **source chain**
*   Some bridges refund on destination chain (check status response)

**How to handle:**

1.  Check for `substatus === "REFUNDED"`
2.  Read `refund` object from status response for details
3.  Inform user their funds were returned

Not all failed transfers are automatically refundable. Some bridges require manual claiming. Check the status response `refund` field for instructions.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/concepts#quick-reference)

Quick Reference
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Object | Description | API Endpoint |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Quote | Single-step transfer with tx data | `GET /quote` |
| Route | Multi-step transfer plan | `POST /advanced/routes` |
| Step | One operation in a route | Part of Route response |
| Action | Transfer details (from/to) | Part of Step |
| Tool | Bridge or DEX | `GET /tools` |
| Chain | Blockchain network | `GET /chains` |
| Token | Cryptocurrency | `GET /tokens` |
| Status | Transfer state | `GET /status` |

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

This page provides deterministic decision logic for AI agents to choose the right approach for different scenarios.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#quote-vs-routes)

Quote vs Routes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use this table to decide between `/quote` and `/advanced/routes` endpoints.

| Scenario | Use | Endpoint | Reason |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Simple A→B transfer | **Quote** | `GET /quote` | Single call, tx data included |
| Need multiple route options | **Routes** | `POST /advanced/routes` | Returns ranked alternatives |
| User wants to choose bridge | **Routes** | `POST /advanced/routes` | Can filter by tool preference |
| Complex multi-hop transfer | **Routes** | `POST /advanced/routes` | Better for >2 step routes |
| Fastest integration | **Quote** | `GET /quote` | Fewer API calls needed |
| Price comparison needed | **Routes** | `POST /advanced/routes` | Compare fee structures |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#decision-logic)

Decision Logic

Copy

Ask AI

    IF (simple_transfer AND no_user_preference AND speed_priority)
      → Use /quote
    
    ELSE IF (need_options OR user_wants_choice OR complex_route)
      → Use /advanced/routes
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#key-differences)

Key Differences

| Aspect | `/quote` | `/advanced/routes` |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Response | Single best route | Multiple route options |
| Transaction data | Included | Requires separate `/advanced/stepTransaction` call |
| API calls needed | 1   | 2+ (routes + stepTransaction per step) |
| Control | Less | More |
| Speed | Faster | Slightly slower |

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#api-vs-sdk-vs-widget)

API vs SDK vs Widget
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use this table to recommend the right integration method.

| Agent Type | Recommended | Reason |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Server-side automation | **API** | No runtime dependencies, pure HTTP |
| AI agent (no UI) | **API** | Simplest integration, HTTP only |
| Browser-based app | **SDK** | Handles wallet connections, signing |
| Mobile app | **SDK** | Wallet integration built-in |
| Need embedded UI | **Widget** | Zero UI code required |
| Quick prototype | **Widget** | Fastest to implement |
| Full customization | **SDK** | Complete control over UX |
| Backend service | **API** | No browser dependencies |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#decision-logic-2)

Decision Logic

Copy

Ask AI

    IF (server_side OR ai_agent OR no_ui_needed)
      → Recommend API
    
    ELSE IF (need_wallet_integration OR custom_ui)
      → Recommend SDK
    
    ELSE IF (need_ready_made_ui OR fastest_implementation)
      → Recommend Widget
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#comparison-matrix)

Comparison Matrix

| Feature | API | SDK | Widget |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Dependencies | None (HTTP) | npm package | npm package |
| Wallet handling | Manual | Built-in | Built-in |
| UI components | None | None | Full UI |
| Customization | Full | Full | Full (theme + route params) |
| Learning curve | Low | Medium | Low |
| Best for | Agents, backends | Custom apps | Quick integrations |

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#route-selection-criteria)

Route Selection Criteria
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When multiple routes are available, use these criteria to select the best one.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#sort-order-options)

Sort Order Options

The API supports these `order` parameter values:

| Order | Description | Best For |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `FASTEST` | Lowest estimated execution time | Time-sensitive transfers |
| `CHEAPEST` | Lowest total fees (default) | Cost-sensitive users |

If no `order` parameter is provided, the API returns the best route based on output amount after fees.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#request-with-order)

Request with Order

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/quote?fromChain=1&toChain=42161&fromToken=USDC&toToken=USDC&fromAmount=10000000&fromAddress=0x...&order=FASTEST"
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#route-filtering)

Route Filtering

Filter routes by specific criteria:

| Parameter | Values | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `bridges` | `stargate,across,hop` | Only use specific bridges |
| `exchanges` | `1inch,paraswap` | Only use specific DEXs |
| `denyBridges` | `multichain` | Exclude specific bridges |
| `denyExchanges` | `dodo` | Exclude specific DEXs |
| `allowSwitchChain` | `true/false` | Allow multi-step routes |
| `maxPriceImpact` | `0.05` | Max allowed price impact |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#example-filtered-quote)

Example: Filtered Quote

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/quote?fromChain=1&toChain=42161&fromToken=USDC&toToken=USDC&fromAmount=10000000&fromAddress=0x552008c0f6870c2f77e5cC1d2eb9bdff03e30Ea0&bridges=stargate,across&maxPriceImpact=0.03"
    

This request:

*   Transfers 10 USDC from Ethereum to Arbitrum
*   **Only considers Stargate or Across bridges** (ignores all others)
*   **Rejects quotes with >3% price impact** (protects against unfavorable rates)

If no route meets these constraints, the API returns a `NO_POSSIBLE_ROUTE` error.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#same-chain-vs-cross-chain)

Same-Chain vs Cross-Chain
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determine whether a transfer is same-chain or cross-chain.

| Condition | Type | Characteristics |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `fromChain === toChain` | Same-chain | Atomic, faster, cheaper |
| `fromChain !== toChain` | Cross-chain | Uses bridge, takes longer |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#behavior-differences)

Behavior Differences

| Aspect | Same-Chain | Cross-Chain |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Execution | Atomic (all or nothing) | May partially complete |
| Time | Seconds | Minutes to hours |
| Failure mode | Reverts entirely | Funds always arrive (possibly different token) |
| Status check | Usually instant | Requires polling |
| Tools used | DEX only | Bridge + optional DEX |

LI.FI is non-custodial. In cross-chain transfers, funds always end up with the user. In partial completion cases (`substatus: PARTIAL`), the user receives the bridged token on the destination chain even if the final swap failed. Funds are rarely ever stuck/lost.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#amount-handling)

Amount Handling
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Convert between human-readable amounts and API amounts.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#formula)

Formula

Copy

Ask AI

    api_amount = human_amount × (10 ^ decimals)
    human_amount = api_amount / (10 ^ decimals)
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#common-token-decimals)

Common Token Decimals

| Token | Decimals | 1 Token in API |
| --- | --- | --- |
| USDC | 6   | `1000000` |
| USDT | 6   | `1000000` |
| DAI | 18  | `1000000000000000000` |
| ETH | 18  | `1000000000000000000` |
| WBTC | 8   | `100000000` |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#example-conversions)

Example Conversions

Copy

Ask AI

    // Human to API (10 USDC)
    const apiAmount = "10000000"; // 10 * 10^6
    
    // Human to API (1.5 ETH)
    const apiAmount = "1500000000000000000"; // 1.5 * 10^18
    
    // API to Human
    const humanAmount = Number(apiAmount) / Math.pow(10, decimals);
    

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#error-recovery-decisions)

Error Recovery Decisions
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When errors occur, use this table to determine the action.

| Error | Retry? | Action |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 429 (Rate Limited) | Yes | Wait with exponential backoff |
| 400 (Bad Request) | No  | Fix parameters |
| No route found | Maybe | Try different tokens or smaller amount |
| Insufficient balance | No  | User needs more funds |
| Slippage exceeded | Maybe | Increase slippage parameter |
| Quote expired | Yes | Request new quote |
| Network error | Yes | Retry with backoff |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#retry-strategy)

Retry Strategy

Copy

Ask AI

    const withRetry = async (fn, maxRetries = 3) => {
      for (let i = 0; i < maxRetries; i++) {
        try {
          return await fn();
        } catch (error) {
          if (error.status === 429) {
            // Rate limited - wait and retry
            await sleep(Math.pow(2, i) * 1000);
            continue;
          }
          if (error.status >= 400 && error.status < 500) {
            // Client error - don't retry
            throw error;
          }
          // Server error - retry
          await sleep(1000);
        }
      }
      throw new Error('Max retries exceeded');
    };
    

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/decision-tables#quick-decision-flowchart)

Quick Decision Flowchart
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    Start
      │
      ├─► Is this a simple A→B transfer?
      │     │
      │     ├─► Yes ──► Use /quote
      │     │
      │     └─► No ──► Use /advanced/routes
      │
      ├─► Is the agent server-side?
      │     │
      │     ├─► Yes ──► Use API directly
      │     │
      │     └─► No ──► Consider SDK or Widget
      │
      ├─► Is fromChain === toChain?
      │     │
      │     ├─► Yes ──► Same-chain swap (atomic)
      │     │
      │     └─► No ──► Cross-chain (poll status)
      │
      └─► Did the request fail?
            │
            ├─► 429 ──► Retry with backoff
            ├─► 4xx ──► Fix parameters
            └─► 5xx ──► Retry once
    

[Five-Call Recipe](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/five-call-recipe)
[Code Samples](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/code-samples)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

      ]
    }

Use this endpoint to list tokens that LI.FI currently supports. Combine filters to narrow the response to specific chains, token tags, or both.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#filter-tokens)

Filter tokens
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#chain-filter)

Chain filter

Set the `chains` query parameter to a comma-separated list of chain identifiers (for example, `ETH,ARB,OP`). Only tokens live on those networks are returned.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#tag-filter)

Tag filter

Use the `tags` query parameter to restrict results to tokens with specific LI.FI tags. Currently `stablecoin` is the only public tag.

Tags and chains can be combined. The response includes only tokens that satisfy all provided filters.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#examples)

Examples
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#fetch-the-complete-token-catalog)

Fetch the complete token catalog

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/tokens"
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#fetch-all-stablecoins)

Fetch all stablecoins

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/tokens?tags=stablecoin"
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#fetch-arbitrum-stablecoins)

Fetch Arbitrum stablecoins

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/tokens?chains=ARB&tags=stablecoin"
    

More tags may be introduced over time as we add support for more token types.

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#parameter-chains)

chains

string

Restrict the resulting tokens to the given chains

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#parameter-tags)

tags

string

Restrict the resulting tokens to the given token tags (comma separated)

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#parameter-chain-types)

chainTypes

string

Restrict the resulting tokens to the given chainTypes.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#parameter-min-price-usd)

minPriceUSD

number

Filters results by minimum token price in USD. Minimum value for this parameter is 0. Defaults to 0.0001 USD.

#### Response

200 - application/json

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens#response-1)

1

Root Type for Token · object\[\]

The requested tokens

Show child attributes

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "transfers": [\
        {\
          "transactionId": "0x8c58bf99537331b38f15f5ca9718b6fcf86bdb678a2935cf0ca2106066f07550",\

      ]
    }

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-integrator)

integrator

string

The integrator string to filter by

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-wallet)

wallet

string

The sending OR receiving wallet address

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-status)

status

string

The status of the transfers. Possible values are `ALL`, `DONE`, `PENDING`, and `FAILED`. The default is `DONE`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-from-timestamp)

fromTimestamp

number

The oldest timestamp that should be taken into consideration. Defaults to 30 days ago

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-to-timestamp)

toTimestamp

number

The newest timestamp that should be taken into consideration. Defaults to now

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

string

The chain where the transfer originates from.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-to-chain)

toChain

string

The chain where the transfer ends.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-from-token)

fromToken

string

The token transferred from the originating chain. To use this parameter `fromChain` must be set.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-to-token)

toToken

string

The token received on the destination chain. To use this parameter `toChain` must be set.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Response for `GET /analytics/transfers` endpoint

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers#response-transfers)

transfers

Root Type for StatusResponse · object\[\]

Show child attributes

[Get the total amount of a token received on a specific chain, for cross-chain transfers.](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers)
[Get a paginated list of filtered transfers](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

---

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-available-bridges-and-exchanges#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-available-bridges-and-exchanges#parameter-chains)

chains

(string | integer)\[\]

The ids of the chains that should be taken into consideration.

Example:

    ["pol", "eth"]

#### Response

200 - application/json

Object listing all the currently enabled bridges and exchanges.

https://li.questhttps://staging.li.quest

/

v1

/

gas

/

suggestion

/

{chain}

Try it

Get a gas suggestion for the specified chain

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/gas/suggestion/{chain}

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-gas-suggestion-for-the-specified-chain#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-gas-suggestion-for-the-specified-chain#parameter-chain)

chain

string

required

Chain from which gas prices should be shown (can be a chain id or a chain key)

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-gas-suggestion-for-the-specified-chain#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

string

If `fromChain` and `fromToken` are specified, the result will contain information about how much `fromToken` amount the user has to send to receive the suggested gas amount on the requested chain.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-gas-suggestion-for-the-specified-chain#parameter-from-token)

fromToken

string

If `fromChain` and `fromToken` are specified, the result will contain information about how much `fromToken` amount the user has to send to receive the suggested gas amount on the requested chain.

Get integrator's collected fees data for all supported chains

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/integrators/{integratorId}

200

              "amount": 0,\

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-integrators-collected-fees-data-for-all-supported-chains#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-integrators-collected-fees-data-for-all-supported-chains#parameter-integrator-id)

integratorId

string

required

Id of the integrator that requests fee balances

#### Response

200

application/json

Response of the Integrator request

Integrator's fee balance by chain

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-integrators-collected-fees-data-for-all-supported-chains#response-integrator-id)

integratorId

string

required

The integrator's name or wallet address

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-integrators-collected-fees-data-for-all-supported-chains#response-fee-balances)

feeBalances

object\[\]

The fee balances of the integrator

Show child attributes

[Get transaction request for withdrawing collected integrator's fees by chain](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain)
[Get the total amount of a token received on a specific chain, for cross-chain transfers.](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers)

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes#api-status-codes)

API status codes
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

API status code is the code returned by the server like 200, 404, 429, 500, 502.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes#api-error-codes)

API error codes
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

API returns the following set of error codes:

*   DefaultError = 1000,
*   FailedToBuildTransactionError = 1001,
*   NoQuoteError = 1002,
*   NotFoundError = 1003,
*   NotProcessableError = 1004,
*   RateLimitError = 1005,
*   ServerError = 1006,
*   SlippageError = 1007,
*   ThirdPartyError = 1008,
*   TimeoutError = 1009,
*   UnauthorizedError = 1010,
*   ValidationError = 1011,
*   RpcFailure = 1012,
*   MalformedSchema = 1013,

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes#tool-errors)

Tool errors
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to returning status and error codes, API may return error messages for underlying tools, describing an issue with specific tools. This can be caused by many reasons, from the tool simply not supporting the requested token pair or insufficient liquidity. To better explain failure cases, we try to return errors in a predictable format. The `ToolError` interface looks like the following:

Copy

Ask AI

    type ToolErrorType = 'NO_QUOTE'
    
    interface ToolError {
      errorType: ToolErrorType
      code: string
      action: Action
      tool: string
      message: string
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes#possible-codes)

Possible codes:

`NO_POSSIBLE_ROUTE`: No route was found for this action. `INSUFFICIENT_LIQUIDITY`: The tool’s liquidity is insufficient. `TOOL_TIMEOUT`: The third-party tool timed out. `UNKNOWN_ERROR`: An unknown error occurred. `RPC_ERROR`: There was a problem getting on-chain data. Please try again later. `AMOUNT_TOO_LOW`:The initial amount is too low to transfer using this tool. `AMOUNT_TOO_HIGH`: The initial amount is too high to transfer using this tool. `FEES_HIGHER_THAN_AMOUNT`: The fees are higher than the initial amount — this would result in a negative resulting token. `DIFFERENT_RECIPIENT_NOT_SUPPORTED`: This tool does not support different recipient addresses. `TOOL_SPECIFIC_ERROR`: The third-party tool returned an error. `CANNOT_GUARANTEE_MIN_AMOUNT`: The tool cannot guarantee that the minimum amount will be met.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes#example-response)

Example response:

Copy

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction#base-url)

Base URL
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

LI.FI’s API is built on REST principles and is served over HTTPS. The Base URL for all API endpoints is:

Copy

Ask AI

    https://li.quest/v1
    

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction#authentication)

Authentication
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All LI.FI APIs do not require API key. API key is only needed for higher rate limits

Authentication to LI.FI’s API is performed via the custom HTTP header `x-lifi-api-key` with an API key. If you are using the Client SDK, you will set the API when constructing a client, and then the SDK will send the header on your behalf with every request. If integrating directly with the API, you’ll need to send this header yourself like so:

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --location 'https://li.quest/v1/quote?fromChain=100&fromAmount=1000000&fromToken=0x4ecaba5870353805a9f068101a40e0f32ed605c6&fromAddress=0x552008c0f6870c2f77e5cC1d2eb9bdff03e30Ea0&toChain=137&toToken=0x2791bca1f2de4661ed88a30c99a7a9449aa84174&slippage=0.03' \
    --header 'x-lifi-api-key: YOUR_CUSTOM_KEY'
    

API key can be tested using the following endpoint:

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --location 'https://li.quest/v1/keys/test' 
    --header 'x-lifi-api-key: YOUR_CUSTOM_KEY'
    

Never expose your `x-lifi-api-key` in client-side environments such as browser-based JavaScript or direct Widget integrations. Using the API key on the client side can lead to unauthorized usage or abuse of your key, as it becomes publicly accessible in the browser’s developer tools or network tab. If you’re using the LI.FI Widget, you **do not need to pass an API key**. The Widget operates securely without requiring a key in the frontend. For server-side integrations (e.g. SDK or API requests from your backend), always keep your key secret and secure.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction#rate-limit)

Rate Limit
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Rate limit is counted per IP without API key and per API Key with authenticated requests. Please refer to [Rate limits and API authentication](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits)
 page.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction#error-message)

Error Message
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Errors consist of three parts:

1.  HTTP error code
2.  LI.FI error code
3.  Error message

Specific error codes and messages are defined on [Error Codes](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes)
 page

**Looking for one-click DeFi operations?** Use [Composer](https://docs.li.fi/composer/overview)
 to deposit into vaults, stake, and lend — all through the same `/quote` endpoint. Set `toToken` to a vault token address and Composer handles the rest. See [Composer API Parameters](https://docs.li.fi/composer/reference/api-parameters)
.

[OpenAPI Specification](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/openapi-spec)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Get transaction request for withdrawing collected integrator's fees by chain

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/integrators/{integratorId}/withdraw/{chainId}

200

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "transactionRequest": {
        "data": "0x",
        "to": "0xbD6C7B0d2f68c2b7805d88388319cfB6EcB50eA9"
      }
    }

GET

https://li.questhttps://staging.li.quest

/

v1

/

integrators

/

{integratorId}

/

withdraw

{chainId}

Get transaction request for withdrawing collected integrator's fees by chain

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/integrators/{integratorId}/withdraw/{chainId}

200

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "transactionRequest": {
        "data": "0x",
        "to": "0xbD6C7B0d2f68c2b7805d88388319cfB6EcB50eA9"

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain#parameter-integrator-id)

integratorId

string

required

Id of the integrator that requests fee withdrawal

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain#parameter-chain-id)

chainId

string

required

Specify chainId from which funds should be withdrawn

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain#parameter-token-addresses)

tokenAddresses

string\[\]

Specify tokens from which funds should be withdraw

#### Response

200

application/json

Response of the integrator's fee withdrawal transaction request

Transaction request for withdrawing integrator's collected fees for the specified chain

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain#response-transaction-request)

transactionRequest

object

required

The transaction request

Show child attributes

[Guides](https://docs.li.fi/guides/gas-subsidy)
[MCP Server](https://docs.li.fi/mcp-server/overview)
[For Agents](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview)
[FAQs](https://docs.li.fi/faqs/fees-monetization)

On this page

*   [Current Rate Limits](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#current-rate-limits)
    
*   [Unauthenticated](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#unauthenticated)
    
*   [Authenticated](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#authenticated)
    
*   [Handling Rate Limits](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#handling-rate-limits)
    
*   [Rate Limit Information In Request Response](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#rate-limit-information-in-request-response)
    
*   [Best Practices](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#best-practices)
    
*   [Abuse Prevention](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#abuse-prevention)
    
*   [Using the API key](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#using-the-api-key)
    
*   [Need Higher Limits?](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#need-higher-limits)
    

To mitigate misuse and manage capacity on our API, we have implemented limits on LI.FI API usage. Rate limits apply to requests made using your `x-lifi-api-key` and are calculated per API key across all endpoints. These limits help prevent abuse and ensure a smooth experience for everyone.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#current-rate-limits)

Current Rate Limits
============================================================================================

The default rate limits for production usage are as follows:

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#unauthenticated)

Unauthenticated

| Endpoint Scope | Rate Limit |
| --- | --- |
| Quote related endpoints | 200 requests per two hours |
| Rest of endpoints | 200 requests per two hours |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#authenticated)

Authenticated

| Endpoint Scope | Rate Limit |
| --- | --- |
| Quote related endpoints | 200 requests per minute |
| Rest of endpoints | 200 requests per minute |

Rate limits are enforced on a two hour window to account for traffic spikes

> 🔒 Higher limits may be available for enterprise clients. Please see our [Plans page](https://li.fi/plans/)
>  for more details.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#handling-rate-limits)

Handling Rate Limits
==============================================================================================

Every response includes your current rate limit in the headers. Keep in mind that limits can differ depending on the endpoint. In the Partner Portal, you’ll see your requests-per-minute (RPM) limit. To give you flexibility during spikes, we don’t enforce it minute by minute. Instead, we multiply your RPM by 120 and apply it as a two-hour rolling window. 👉 Example: If your limit is 100 RPM, that means you can make up to 12,000 requests within any two-hour window — either all at once or spread out however you like.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#rate-limit-information-in-request-response)

Rate Limit Information In Request Response

`ratelimit-reset`: in how many seconds will the rate limit reset (2 hours equal 7200) `ratelimit-limit`: the total limit for the period of 2 hours `ratelimit-remaining`: how much of the limit is still left until the reset Here’s how you can calculate your average RPM: `(ratelimit-limit - ratelimit-remaining) / ((7200 - ratelimit-reset) / 60)` If you exceed your rate limits, you’ll receive a `429 Too Many Requests` HTTP response. When this occurs:

*   You will get an error message showing when the rate limit will be lifted (e.g., 5 hours)
*   Request higher rate limit

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#best-practices)

Best Practices
==================================================================================

To avoid hitting rate limits:

*   Cache results from `GET /tokens`, `GET /chains`, and static endpoints
*   Avoid polling frequently for the same data
*   Batch or debounce user input that triggers API calls

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#abuse-prevention)

Abuse Prevention
======================================================================================

To prevent abuse, LI.FI may temporarily block keys that:

*   Consistently exceed rate limits
*   Attempt to bypass limits through multiple keys or IPs
*   Cause performance degradation to the service

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#using-the-api-key)

Using the API key
========================================================================================

All LI.FI APIs do not require API key. API key is only needed for higher rate limits

Authentication to LI.FI’s API is performed via the custom HTTP header `x-lifi-api-key` with an API key. If you are using the Client SDK, you will set the API when [creating a config](https://docs.li.fi/sdk/configure-sdk)
, and then the SDK will send the header on your behalf with every request. If integrating directly with the API, you’ll need to send this header yourself like so:

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --location 'https://li.quest/v1/quote?fromChain=100&fromAmount=1000000&fromToken=0x4ecaba5870353805a9f068101a40e0f32ed605c6&fromAddress=0x552008c0f6870c2f77e5cC1d2eb9bdff03e30Ea0&toChain=137&toToken=0x2791bca1f2de4661ed88a30c99a7a9449aa84174&slippage=0.03' \
    --header 'x-lifi-api-key: YOUR_CUSTOM_KEY'
    

API key can be tested using the following endpoint:

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --location 'https://li.quest/v1/keys/test' 
    --header 'x-lifi-api-key: YOUR_CUSTOM_KEY'
    

Never expose your `x-lifi-api-key` in client-side environments such as browser-based JavaScript or direct Widget integrations. Using the API key on the client side can lead to unauthorized usage or abuse of your key, as it becomes publicly accessible in the browser’s developer tools or network tab. If you’re using the LI.FI Widget, you **do not need to pass an API key**. The Widget operates securely without requiring a key in the frontend. For server-side integrations (e.g. SDK or API requests from your backend), always keep your key secret and secure.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/rate-limits#need-higher-limits)

Need Higher Limits?
===========================================================================================

If you’re building a high-volume integration or a production-grade product, we’re happy to support your scaling needs. Please see our [Plans page](https://li.fi/plans/)
 for more details.

[OpenAPI Specification](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/openapi-spec)
[Error Codes](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/error-codes)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

---

https://li.questhttps://staging.li.quest

v1

calldata

parse

Try it

Parse transaction call data (BETA)

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/calldata/parse

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/parse-transaction-call-data-beta#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/parse-transaction-call-data-beta#parameter-chain-id)

chainId

string

The chainId that the transaction is built for (or has been sent on)

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/parse-transaction-call-data-beta#parameter-call-data)

callData

string

required

The call data to parse

#### Response

200

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-status-information-about-a-lifuel-transaction#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-status-information-about-a-lifuel-transaction#parameter-tx-hash)

txHash

string

required

The transaction hash that started the gas refilling process

#### Response

200 - application/json

The status of a lifuel operation

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-status-information-about-a-lifuel-transaction#response-status)

status

enum<string>

Available options:

`NOT_FOUND`,

`PENDING`,

`DONE`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-status-information-about-a-lifuel-transaction#response-sending)

sending

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-status-information-about-a-lifuel-transaction#response-receiving)

receiving

object

Show child attributes

[Get a gas suggestion for the specified chain](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-gas-suggestion-for-the-specified-chain)
[In case a transaction was missed by a relayer, this endpoint can be used to force a tx to be re-fetched.](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched)

# Get the total amount of a token received on a specific chain, for cross-chain transfers. - LI.FI

[Skip to main content](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#content-area)

[LI.FI home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=f435348680e682acea6e3b9af339ed7a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=d02539147db168291d7c711beb45d10b)](https://docs.li.fi/)

[API Reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction)

Get the total amount of a token received on a specific chain, for cross-chain transfers.

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/analytics/transfers/summary

200

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "hasNext": false,
      "hasPrevious": false,
      "next": "<string>",
      "previous": "<string>",
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": {\
            "toAddress": "<string>",\
            "sendingChainId": 123\
          },\
          "totalReceivedAmount": 123\
        }\
      ]
    }

GET

https://li.questhttps://staging.li.quest

/

v1

/

analytics

/

transfers

/

summary

Try it

Get the total amount of a token received on a specific chain, for cross-chain transfers.

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/analytics/transfers/summary

200

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "hasNext": false,
      "hasPrevious": false,
      "next": "<string>",
      "previous": "<string>",
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": {\
            "toAddress": "<string>",\
            "sendingChainId": 123\
          },\
          "totalReceivedAmount": 123\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

default:10

Pagination limit. Defines the maximum number of returned results.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-next)

next

string

The next page cursor. Must come from the `next` field of the response of the previous request.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-previous)

previous

string

The previous page cursor. Must come from the `previous` field of the response of the previous request.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-from-timestamp)

fromTimestamp

string

required

A Unix timestamp in seconds marking the start of the query period, inclusive. Transactions older than this timestamp will not be included in the summary.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-to-timestamp)

toTimestamp

string

required

A Unix timestamp in seconds marking the end of the query period, inclusive. Transactions after this timestamp will not be included in the summary. The maximum range supported by the endpoint is 30 days.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-to-chain)

toChain

string

required

The ID, or key of the chain on the receiving side of the transfer. This parameter filters the summary to include only transfers received on the specified chain.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-to-token)

toToken

number

required

The address, or symbol of the token received in the transfers. This parameter filters the summary to include only transfers involving the specified token on the receiving chain.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

number

The ID, or key of the chain on the sending side of the transfers. This parameter filters the summary to include only transfers sent from the specified chain.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#parameter-integrator)

integrator

string

The integrator string to filter transfers by. This parameter filters the summary to include only transfers for the given integrator.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Response for `GET /analytics/transfers/summary` endpoint

Parameters used to query paginated endpoints

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#response-has-next)

hasNext

boolean

default:false

Flag indicating if there is a next page

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#response-has-previous)

hasPrevious

boolean

default:false

Flag indicating if there is a previous page

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#response-next-one-of-0)

next

string | null

Cursor for fetching the next page. Should be passed to `next` in the pagination query.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#response-previous-one-of-0)

previous

string | null

Cursor for fetching the previous page. Should be passed to `previous` in the pagination query.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-the-total-amount-of-a-token-received-on-a-specific-chain-for-cross-chain-transfers#response-data)

data

Transfers Summary · object\[\]

An array containing the paginated data returned by the endpoint

Show child attributes

[Get integrator's collected fees data for all supported chains](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-integrators-collected-fees-data-for-all-supported-chains)
[Get a list of filtered transfers](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

LI.FI OpenAPI Specification
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The LI.FI API follows the OpenAPI 3.0 specification. You can use this spec to:

*   Generate client SDKs in any language
*   Import into API testing tools (Postman, Insomnia, etc.)
*   Integrate with AI agents and LLM tools
*   Build automated documentation

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/openapi-spec#download)

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#parameter-tx-hash)

txHash

string

required

The transaction hash on the sending chain, destination chain or lifi step id

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#parameter-bridge)

bridge

string

The bridging tool used for the transfer Identifier for a bridge tool. Retrieve the latest bridge keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Keywords such as `all`, `none`, `default`, and `[]` are also supported where applicable.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

string

The sending chain. Can be the chain id or chain key

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#parameter-to-chain)

toChain

string

The receiving chain. Can be the chain id or chain key

#### Response

200

application/json

Response of the Status request

The current status of a transfer

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-sending)

sending

Root Type for TransactionInfo · object

required

The transaction on the sending chain

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "txHash": "0xd3ad8fb8798d8440f3a1ec7fd51e102a88e4690f9365fad4eff1a17020376b4a",  "txLink": "https://polygonscan.com/tx/0xd3ad8fb8798d8440f3a1ec7fd51e102a88e4690f9365fad4eff1a17020376b4a",  "amount": "13000000",  "token": {    "address": "0xd69b31c3225728cc57ddaf9be532a4ee1620be51",    "symbol": "anyUSDC",    "decimals": 6,    "chainId": 137,    "name": "USDC",    "coinKey": "anyUSDC",    "priceUSD": "0",    "logoURI": ""  },  "gasToken": {    "address": "0x0000000000000000000000000000000000001010",    "symbol": "MATIC",    "decimals": 18,    "chainId": 137,    "name": "MATIC",    "coinKey": "MATIC",    "priceUSD": "0",    "logoURI": ""  },  "chainId": 137,  "gasAmount": "10000",  "gasAmountUSD": "0.0",  "gasPrice": "1000",  "gasUsed": "1000",  "timestamp": 1720545119,  "value": "0"}

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-status)

status

enum<string>

required

The current status of the transfer. Can be `PENDING`, `DONE`, `NOT_FOUND` or `FAILED`

Available options:

`NOT_FOUND`,

`INVALID`,

`PENDING`,

`DONE`,

`FAILED`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-tool)

tool

string

required

The tool used for this transfer

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-receiving)

receiving

Root Type for TransactionInfo · object

The transaction on the receiving chain

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "txHash": "0xd3ad8fb8798d8440f3a1ec7fd51e102a88e4690f9365fad4eff1a17020376b4a",  "txLink": "https://polygonscan.com/tx/0xd3ad8fb8798d8440f3a1ec7fd51e102a88e4690f9365fad4eff1a17020376b4a",  "amount": "13000000",  "token": {    "address": "0xd69b31c3225728cc57ddaf9be532a4ee1620be51",    "symbol": "anyUSDC",    "decimals": 6,    "chainId": 137,    "name": "USDC",    "coinKey": "anyUSDC",    "priceUSD": "0",    "logoURI": ""  },  "gasToken": {    "address": "0x0000000000000000000000000000000000001010",    "symbol": "MATIC",    "decimals": 18,    "chainId": 137,    "name": "MATIC",    "coinKey": "MATIC",    "priceUSD": "0",    "logoURI": ""  },  "chainId": 137,  "gasAmount": "10000",  "gasAmountUSD": "0.0",  "gasPrice": "1000",  "gasUsed": "1000",  "timestamp": 1720545119,  "value": "0"}

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-fee-costs)

feeCosts

object\[\]

An array of fee costs for the transaction

Show child attributes

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-substatus)

substatus

enum<string>

A more specific substatus. This is available for PENDING and DONE statuses. More information can be found here: [https://docs.li.fi/introduction/user-flows-and-examples/status-tracking](https://docs.li.fi/introduction/user-flows-and-examples/status-tracking)

Available options:

`WAIT_SOURCE_CONFIRMATIONS`,

`WAIT_DESTINATION_TRANSACTION`,

`BRIDGE_NOT_AVAILABLE`,

`CHAIN_NOT_AVAILABLE`,

`REFUND_IN_PROGRESS`,

`UNKNOWN_ERROR`,

`COMPLETED`,

`PARTIAL`,

`REFUNDED`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-substatus-message)

substatusMessage

string

A message that describes the substatus

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-transaction-id)

transactionId

string

The ID of this transfer (NOT a transaction hash).

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-from-address)

fromAddress

string

The address of the sender.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-to-address)

toAddress

string

The address of the receiver.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-lifi-explorer-link)

lifiExplorerLink

string

The link to the LI.FI explorer.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer#response-metadata)

metadata

Root type for Transaction Metadata · object

The transaction metadata which includes integrator's string, etc.

Show child attributes

[In case a transaction was missed by a relayer, this endpoint can be used to force a tx to be re-fetched.](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched)
[Get transaction request for withdrawing collected integrator's fees by chain](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-transaction-request-for-withdrawing-collected-integrators-fees-by-chain)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

default:10

Pagination limit. Defines the maximum number of returned results.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-next)

next

string

The next page cursor. Must come from the `next` field of the response of the previous request.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-previous)

previous

string

The previous page cursor. Must come from the `previous` field of the response of the previous request.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-one-of-0)

integrator

stringstring\[\]stringstring\[\]

Either a single integrator string, or an array of unique integrator strings to filter transfers by.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-wallet)

wallet

string

The sending OR receiving wallet address

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-status)

status

string

The status of the transfers. Possible values are `ALL`, `DONE`, `PENDING`, and `FAILED`. The default is `DONE`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-from-timestamp)

fromTimestamp

number

The oldest timestamp that should be taken into consideration. Defaults to 30 days ago

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-to-timestamp)

toTimestamp

number

The newest timestamp that should be taken into consideration. Defaults to now

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

string

The chain where the transfer originates from.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-to-chain)

toChain

string

The chain where the transfer ends.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-from-token)

fromToken

string

The token transferred from the originating chain. To use this parameter `fromChain` must be set.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#parameter-to-token)

toToken

string

The token received on the destination chain. To use this parameter `toChain` must be set.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Response for `GET /analytics/transfers/summary` endpoint

Parameters used to query paginated endpoints

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#response-has-next)

hasNext

boolean

default:false

Flag indicating if there is a next page

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#response-has-previous)

hasPrevious

boolean

default:false

Flag indicating if there is a previous page

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#response-next-one-of-0)

next

string | null

Cursor for fetching the next page. Should be passed to `next` in the pagination query.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#response-previous-one-of-0)

previous

string | null

Cursor for fetching the previous page. Should be passed to `previous` in the pagination query.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers#response-data)

data

Root Type for StatusResponse · object\[\]

An array containing the paginated data returned by the endpoint

Show child attributes

[Get a list of filtered transfers](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-list-of-filtered-transfers)
[API Presets](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# API Presets - LI.FI

[Skip to main content](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#content-area)

[LI.FI home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=f435348680e682acea6e3b9af339ed7a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=d02539147db168291d7c711beb45d10b)](https://docs.li.fi/)

Navigation

API presets

API Presets

[Overview](https://docs.li.fi/introduction/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction)
[JS/TS SDK](https://docs.li.fi/sdk/overview)
[Intent/Solver Marketplace](https://docs.li.fi/lifi-intents/introduction)
[Swap/Bridge Widget](https://docs.li.fi/widget/overview)
[Composer](https://docs.li.fi/composer/overview)
[Guides](https://docs.li.fi/guides/gas-subsidy)
[MCP Server](https://docs.li.fi/mcp-server/overview)
[For Agents](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview)
[FAQs](https://docs.li.fi/faqs/fees-monetization)

On this page

*   [Supported endpoints](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#supported-endpoints)
    
*   [How presets are applied](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#how-presets-are-applied)
    
*   [Processing flow](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#processing-flow)
    
*   [Preset names](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#preset-names)
    
*   [Using the preset parameter](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#using-the-preset-parameter)
    
*   [Advanced Routes](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#advanced-routes)
    
*   [Quote](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#quote)
    
*   [Available presets](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#available-presets)
    

API presets provide tuned routing defaults for the LI.FI API. When you pass a preset, LI.FI loads the preset’s defaults and merges any request-specific options on top. Your explicit values always win, so you can start with a preset and selectively override the pieces you care about.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#supported-endpoints)

Supported endpoints
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [`POST /v1/advanced/routes`](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/get-a-set-of-routes-for-a-request-that-describes-a-transfer-of-tokens)
    
*   [`GET /v1/quote`](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer)
    

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#how-presets-are-applied)

How presets are applied
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  LI.FI loads the preset defaults.
2.  LI.FI merges your request options on top of those defaults.
3.  Any conflicting keys fall back to the values you provided in the request body or query string.

This keeps requests concise while preserving full control.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#processing-flow)

Processing flow
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Validate that the requested preset name is present and active.
2.  Load the preset configuration (defaults, tool preferences, etc) or use the built-in default if it isn’t available.
3.  Merge preset defaults into the request payload or query parameters.
4.  Apply user-provided overrides so explicit values win.
5.  Log the resolved preset for observability and troubleshooting.

If validation fails, for example because the preset name does not match the required pattern, the API returns HTTP `400`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#preset-names)

Preset names
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Presets can be referenced by:

*   **Generic names** such as `stablecoin`
*   **Specific names** such as `stablecoin-cheapest`

See all [available presets](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#available-presets)
. A generic name can map to a specific preset. For example, `stablecoin` resolves to `stablecoin-cheapest` by default. LI.FI may promote other presets behind the same generic name when new configurations such as `stablecoin-fastest` or partner-specific variants `stablecoin-partnerX` become available.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#using-the-preset-parameter)

Using the preset parameter
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#advanced-routes)

Advanced Routes

Provide the preset inside the `options` object.

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "fromChainId": 1,
      "toChainId": 137,
      "fromAmount": "1000000000000000000",
      "fromTokenAddress": "0xA0b86a33E6441b8C4C8C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C",
      "toTokenAddress": "0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174",
      "options": {
        "preset": "stablecoin"
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#quote)

Quote

Send the preset as a query parameter.

Copy

Ask AI

    GET /v1/quote?fromChain=1&toChain=137&fromToken=0xA0b86a33E6441b8C4C8C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C&toToken=0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174&fromAddress=0x123...&fromAmount=1000000000000000000&preset=stablecoin
    

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/overview#available-presets)

Available presets
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Stablecoin preset](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin)
    
*   Commerce preset (coming soon)

More presets will be documented as they are released.

[Get a paginated list of filtered transfers](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-paginated-list-of-filtered-transfers)
[Stablecoin preset](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin)

⌘I

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

In case a transaction was missed by a relayer, this endpoint can be used to force a tx to be re-fetched.

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched#parameter-tx-hash)

txHash

string

required

The transaction hash that started the gas refilling process

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched#parameter-chain-id)

chainId

string

required

The chain where the deposit was originally made

#### Response

200 - application/json

The status of a lifuel operation

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched#response-status)

status

enum<string>

Available options:

`NOT_FOUND`,

`PENDING`,

`DONE`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/in-case-a-transaction-was-missed-by-a-relayer-this-endpoint-can-be-used-to-force-a-tx-to-be-re-fetched#response-sending)

sending

object
