[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------

LI.FI provides cross-chain swaps and bridging across 58 blockchains (EVM, Solana, Bitcoin, SUI), aggregating 27 bridges and 31 exchanges. This page is designed as the entry point for AI agents that need to execute token transfers, check transaction status, or query supported chains and tokens.

**Machine-readable resources:**

*   [llms.txt](https://docs.li.fi/llms.txt)
     - Structured overview for LLM consumption
*   [OpenAPI Spec](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lifinance/public-docs/main/openapi.yaml)
     - Full API specification
*   [AI Plugin](https://docs.li.fi/.well-known/ai-plugin.json)
     - Standard discovery format

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#when-to-use-what)

When to Use What
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Use Case | Recommended | Why |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Execute transfers from backend | **API** | Direct HTTP calls, full control |
| Build frontend with swaps | **SDK** | Handles wallets, signing, execution |
| Embed ready-made UI | **Widget** | Zero-code, instant deployment |
| AI agent integration | **API** | Simple HTTP, no dependencies |

For AI agents, the **REST API** is recommended since it requires only HTTP calls without additional dependencies.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#minimal-endpoint-set)

Minimal Endpoint Set
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These 5 endpoints cover most agent use cases:

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#1-get-a-quote)

1\. Get a Quote

Returns a ready-to-execute transaction for transferring tokens.

Copy

Ask AI

    GET https://li.quest/v1/quote?fromChain=1&toChain=42161&fromToken=USDC&toToken=USDC&fromAmount=1000000&fromAddress=0x...
    

**Required parameters:**

*   `fromChain` - Source chain ID (e.g., `1` for Ethereum)
*   `toChain` - Destination chain ID (e.g., `42161` for Arbitrum)
*   `fromToken` - Token symbol or address
*   `toToken` - Token symbol or address
*   `fromAmount` - Amount in smallest unit (wei)
*   `fromAddress` - Sender wallet address

**Returns:** Quote object with `transactionRequest` ready for signing.[Full Quote Documentation\
------------------------\
\
See all parameters and response schema](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#2-check-transfer-status)

2\. Check Transfer Status

Poll this endpoint to track cross-chain transfer progress.

Copy

Ask AI

    GET https://li.quest/v1/status?txHash=0x...
    

**Required parameters:**

*   `txHash` - Transaction hash from the source chain

**Optional parameters (recommended for faster response):**

*   `fromChain` - Source chain ID
*   `toChain` - Destination chain ID
*   `bridge` - Bridge name from the quote (e.g., `stargate`)

**Returns:** Status object with `status` field: `NOT_FOUND`, `PENDING`, `DONE`, or `FAILED`.[Full Status Documentation\
-------------------------\
\
See all status values and substatus details](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/check-the-status-of-a-cross-chain-transfer)

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#3-list-supported-chains)

3\. List Supported Chains

Get all chains LI.FI supports.

Copy

Ask AI

    GET https://li.quest/v1/chains
    

**Optional parameters:**

*   `chainTypes` - Filter by type: `EVM`, `SVM`, `UTXO`, `MVM`

**Returns:** Array of chain objects with `id`, `key`, `name`, `chainType`.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#4-list-supported-tokens)

4\. List Supported Tokens

Get tokens available for a specific chain.

Copy

Ask AI

    GET https://li.quest/v1/tokens?chains=1,42161
    

**Required parameters:**

*   `chains` - Comma-separated chain IDs

**Returns:** Map of chain IDs to token arrays with `address`, `symbol`, `decimals`.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#5-list-available-tools)

5\. List Available Tools

Get bridges and DEXs available for routing.

Copy

Ask AI

    GET https://li.quest/v1/tools
    

**Returns:** Object with `bridges` and `exchanges` arrays, each containing `key`, `name`, and `supportedChains`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#decision-rules)

Decision Rules
------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#choosing-between-quote-and-routes)

Choosing Between Quote and Routes

*   **Use `/quote`** for simple transfers - returns single best route with transaction data
*   **Use `/advanced/routes`** when you need multiple options or complex multi-step transfers

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#handling-status-responses)

Handling Status Responses

Copy

Ask AI

    Status: PENDING
    ├── Keep polling every 10-30 seconds
    └── Check substatus for detailed progress
    
    Status: DONE
    ├── substatus: COMPLETED → Transfer successful
    ├── substatus: PARTIAL → User received different token (still success)
    └── substatus: REFUNDED → Tokens returned to sender
    
    Status: FAILED
    └── Check error message, may need user intervention
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#error-handling)

Error Handling

1.  **Rate limited (429):** Back off and retry with exponential delay
2.  **No route found:** Try different token pairs or reduce amount
3.  **Insufficient balance:** Verify user has enough tokens + gas
4.  **Slippage exceeded:** Increase `slippage` parameter (default: 0.005)

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#common-chain-ids)

Common Chain IDs
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Chain | ID  | Key |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Ethereum | 1   | `eth` |
| Arbitrum | 42161 | `arb` |
| Optimism | 10  | `opt` |
| Base | 8453 | `bas` |
| Polygon | 137 | `pol` |
| BSC | 56  | `bsc` |
| Avalanche | 43114 | `ava` |
| Solana | 1151111081099710 | `sol` |

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview#common-token-addresses)

Common Token Addresses
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Token | Ethereum | Arbitrum | Base |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| USDC | `0xA0b86991c6218b36c1d19D4a2e9Eb0cE3606eB48` | `0xaf88d065e77c8cC2239327C5EDb3A432268e5831` | `0x833589fCD6eDb6E08f4c7C32D4f71b54bdA02913` |
| USDT | `0xdAC17F958D2ee523a2206206994597C13D831ec7` | `0xFd086bC7CD5C481DCC9C85ebE478A1C0b69FCbb9` | \-  |
| WETH | `0xC02aaA39b223FE8D0A0e5C4F27eAD9083C756Cc2` | `0x82aF49447D8a07e3bd95BD0d56f35241523fBab1` | `0x4200000000000000000000000000000000000006` |

Use token symbols (`USDC`, `ETH`) for convenience - the API resolves them to addresses automatically.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/code-samples#node-js-api-only)

Node.js (API Only)
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A complete example using only HTTP requests - no SDK required.

Copy

Ask AI

    // lifi-agent.js
    // Run with: node lifi-agent.js
    
    const LIFI_API = 'https://li.quest/v1';
    
    // Optional: Set API key for higher rate limits
    const API_KEY = process.env.LIFI_API_KEY || '';
    
    const headers = {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      ...(API_KEY && { 'x-lifi-api-key': API_KEY })
    };
    
    // Helper: Sleep for exponential backoff
    const sleep = (ms) => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
    
    // Helper: Fetch with retry and backoff
    async function fetchWithRetry(url, options = {}, maxRetries = 3) {
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt < maxRetries; attempt++) {
        try {
          const response = await fetch(url, { ...options, headers });
          
          if (response.status === 429) {
            // Rate limited - exponential backoff
            const waitTime = Math.pow(2, attempt) * 1000;
            console.log(`Rate limited. Waiting ${waitTime}ms...`);
            await sleep(waitTime);
            continue;
          }
          
          if (!response.ok) {
            const error = await response.json();
            throw new Error(`API Error: ${error.message || response.statusText}`);
          }
          
          return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
          if (attempt === maxRetries - 1) throw error;
          await sleep(1000);
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Step 1: Get supported chains
    async function getChains(chainTypes = 'EVM') {
      const url = `${LIFI_API}/chains?chainTypes=${chainTypes}`;
      const data = await fetchWithRetry(url);
      return data.chains;
    }
    
    // Step 2: Get tokens for chains
    async function getTokens(chainIds) {
      const url = `${LIFI_API}/tokens?chains=${chainIds.join(',')}`;
      const data = await fetchWithRetry(url);
      return data.tokens;
    }
    
    // Step 3: Get a quote
    async function getQuote(params) {
      const {
        fromChain,
        toChain,
        fromToken,
        toToken,
        fromAmount,
        fromAddress,
        slippage = 0.005
      } = params;
      
      const url = new URL(`${LIFI_API}/quote`);
      url.searchParams.set('fromChain', fromChain);
      url.searchParams.set('toChain', toChain);
      url.searchParams.set('fromToken', fromToken);
      url.searchParams.set('toToken', toToken);
      url.searchParams.set('fromAmount', fromAmount);
      url.searchParams.set('fromAddress', fromAddress);
      url.searchParams.set('slippage', slippage);
      
      return await fetchWithRetry(url.toString());
    }
    
    // Step 4: Check transfer status
    async function getStatus(txHash, bridge, fromChain, toChain) {
      const url = `${LIFI_API}/status?txHash=${txHash}&bridge=${bridge}&fromChain=${fromChain}&toChain=${toChain}`;
      return await fetchWithRetry(url);
    }
    
    // Step 5: Poll status until complete
    async function pollStatus(txHash, bridge, fromChain, toChain, maxAttempts = 60) {
      console.log('Polling transfer status...');
      
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt < maxAttempts; attempt++) {
        const status = await getStatus(txHash, bridge, fromChain, toChain);
        
        console.log(`Status: ${status.status} (${status.substatus || 'no substatus'})`);
        
        if (status.status === 'DONE') {
          if (status.substatus === 'COMPLETED') {
            console.log('Transfer completed successfully!');
            return { success: true, status };
          }
          if (status.substatus === 'PARTIAL') {
            console.log('Transfer completed with different token');
            return { success: true, partial: true, status };
          }
          if (status.substatus === 'REFUNDED') {
            console.log('Transfer failed - tokens refunded');
            return { success: false, refunded: true, status };
          }
        }
        
        if (status.status === 'FAILED') {
          console.log('Transfer failed');
          return { success: false, status };
        }
        
        // Wait 10 seconds before next poll
        await sleep(10000);
      }
      
      throw new Error('Status polling timeout');
    }
    
    // Main execution flow
    async function executeTransfer(params) {
      console.log('Getting quote...');
      const quote = await getQuote(params);
      
      console.log(`Quote received: ${quote.tool}`);
      console.log(`Expected output: ${quote.estimate.toAmount}`);
      console.log(`Minimum output: ${quote.estimate.toAmountMin}`);
      
      // Here you would:
      // 1. Check if approval is needed (for ERC20 tokens)
      // 2. Send approval transaction if needed
      // 3. Send the main transaction using quote.transactionRequest
      // 4. Get the txHash from the transaction receipt
      
      console.log('\nTransaction request ready:');
      console.log(JSON.stringify(quote.transactionRequest, null, 2));
      
      return quote;
    }
    
    // Example usage
    async function main() {
      try {
        // Get available chains
        const chains = await getChains();
        console.log(`Found ${chains.length} chains`);
        
        // Get quote for 10 USDC from Ethereum to Arbitrum
        const quote = await executeTransfer({
          fromChain: 1,
          toChain: 42161,
          fromToken: 'USDC',
          toToken: 'USDC',
          fromAmount: '10000000', // 10 USDC (6 decimals)
          fromAddress: '0x552008c0f6870c2f77e5cC1d2eb9bdff03e30Ea0' // Replace with actual address
        });
        
        // After executing the transaction, poll for status:
        // const result = await pollStatus(txHash, quote.tool, 1, 42161);
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error:', error.message);
      }
    }
    
    main();

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/code-samples#node-js-with-sdk)

Node.js (with SDK)
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Using the LI.FI SDK for full execution support.

Copy

Ask AI

    // lifi-sdk-agent.js
    // Install: npm install @lifi/sdk viem
    // Run with: node lifi-sdk-agent.js
    
    import { createConfig, getQuote, executeRoute, convertQuoteToRoute } from '@lifi/sdk';
    import { createWalletClient, http } from 'viem';
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from 'viem/accounts';
    import { mainnet, arbitrum } from 'viem/chains';
    
    // Configuration
    const PRIVATE_KEY = process.env.PRIVATE_KEY; // Never hardcode!
    const INTEGRATOR_NAME = 'your-agent-name';
    
    // Initialize SDK
    createConfig({
      integrator: INTEGRATOR_NAME,
      // Optional: API key for higher rate limits
      // apiKey: process.env.LIFI_API_KEY,
    });
    
    // Create wallet client
    const account = privateKeyToAccount(PRIVATE_KEY);
    const walletClient = createWalletClient({
      account,
      chain: mainnet,
      transport: http(),
    });
    
    // Get a quote
    async function fetchQuote(params) {
      const quote = await getQuote({
        fromChain: params.fromChain,
        toChain: params.toChain,
        fromToken: params.fromToken,
        toToken: params.toToken,
        fromAmount: params.fromAmount,
        fromAddress: account.address,
      });
      
      return quote;
    }
    
    // Execute the transfer
    async function executeTransfer(quote) {
      console.log('Executing transfer...');
      
      // Convert quote to route format for execution
      const route = convertQuoteToRoute(quote);
      
      const result = await executeRoute(route, {
        // Update hook called on each status change
        updateRouteHook: (updatedRoute) => {
          console.log('Route updated:', updatedRoute.id);
          const step = updatedRoute.steps[0];
          if (step?.execution) {
            console.log(`Execution status: ${step.execution.status}`);
          }
        },
      });
      
      return result;
    }
    
    // Main flow
    async function main() {
      try {
        console.log(`Wallet address: ${account.address}`);
        
        // Get quote
        const quote = await fetchQuote({
          fromChain: 1,        // Ethereum
          toChain: 42161,      // Arbitrum
          fromToken: 'USDC',
          toToken: 'USDC',
          fromAmount: '10000000', // 10 USDC
        });
        
        console.log('Quote received:');
        console.log(`- Tool: ${quote.tool}`);
        console.log(`- Expected: ${quote.estimate.toAmount}`);
        console.log(`- Minimum: ${quote.estimate.toAmountMin}`);
        
        // Execute (uncomment to run actual transfer)
        // const result = await executeTransfer(quote);
        // console.log('Transfer complete:', result);
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error:', error.message);
      }
    }
    
    main();
    

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/code-samples#python-api-only)

Python (API Only)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Complete Python example using only HTTP requests.

Copy

Ask AI

    # lifi_agent.py
    # Install: pip install requests
    # Run with: python lifi_agent.py
    
    import os
    import time
    import requests
    from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
    
    LIFI_API = "https://li.quest/v1"
    API_KEY = os.environ.get("LIFI_API_KEY", "")
    
    def get_headers() -> Dict[str, str]:
        headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
        if API_KEY:
            headers["x-lifi-api-key"] = API_KEY
        return headers
    
    
    def fetch_with_retry(url: str, max_retries: int = 3) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Fetch with exponential backoff for rate limiting."""
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                response = requests.get(url, headers=get_headers())
                
                if response.status_code == 429:
                    wait_time = (2 ** attempt)
                    print(f"Rate limited. Waiting {wait_time}s...")
                    time.sleep(wait_time)
                    continue
                
                response.raise_for_status()
                return response.json()
                
            except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
                if attempt == max_retries - 1:
                    raise
                time.sleep(1)
        
        raise Exception("Max retries exceeded")
    
    
    def get_chains(chain_types: str = "EVM") -> List[Dict]:
        """Get supported chains."""
        url = f"{LIFI_API}/chains?chainTypes={chain_types}"
        data = fetch_with_retry(url)
        return data["chains"]
    
    
    def get_tokens(chain_ids: List[int]) -> Dict[str, List[Dict]]:
        """Get tokens for specified chains."""
        chains_param = ",".join(str(c) for c in chain_ids)
        url = f"{LIFI_API}/tokens?chains={chains_param}"
        data = fetch_with_retry(url)
        return data["tokens"]
    
    
    def get_quote(
        from_chain: int,
        to_chain: int,
        from_token: str,
        to_token: str,
        from_amount: str,
        from_address: str,
        slippage: float = 0.005
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get a quote for token transfer."""
        params = {
            "fromChain": from_chain,
            "toChain": to_chain,
            "fromToken": from_token,
            "toToken": to_token,
            "fromAmount": from_amount,
            "fromAddress": from_address,
            "slippage": slippage
        }
        
        url = f"{LIFI_API}/quote?" + "&".join(f"{k}={v}" for k, v in params.items())
        return fetch_with_retry(url)
    
    
    def get_status(
        tx_hash: str,
        bridge: str,
        from_chain: int,
        to_chain: int
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Check transfer status."""
        url = f"{LIFI_API}/status?txHash={tx_hash}&bridge={bridge}&fromChain={from_chain}&toChain={to_chain}"
        return fetch_with_retry(url)
    
    
    def poll_status(
        tx_hash: str,
        bridge: str,
        from_chain: int,
        to_chain: int,
        max_attempts: int = 60,
        poll_interval: int = 10
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Poll status until transfer completes."""
        print("Polling transfer status...")
        
        for attempt in range(max_attempts):
            status = get_status(tx_hash, bridge, from_chain, to_chain)
            
            status_str = status.get("status", "UNKNOWN")
            substatus_str = status.get("substatus", "")
            print(f"Status: {status_str} ({substatus_str})")
            
            if status_str == "DONE":
                if substatus_str == "COMPLETED":
                    print("Transfer completed successfully!")
                    return {"success": True, "status": status}
                elif substatus_str == "PARTIAL":
                    print("Transfer completed with different token")
                    return {"success": True, "partial": True, "status": status}
                elif substatus_str == "REFUNDED":
                    print("Transfer failed - tokens refunded")
                    return {"success": False, "refunded": True, "status": status}
            
            if status_str == "FAILED":
                print("Transfer failed")
                return {"success": False, "status": status}
            
            time.sleep(poll_interval)
        
        raise Exception("Status polling timeout")
    
    
    def execute_transfer(
        from_chain: int,
        to_chain: int,
        from_token: str,
        to_token: str,
        from_amount: str,
        from_address: str
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get quote and prepare for execution."""
        print("Getting quote...")
        quote = get_quote(
            from_chain=from_chain,
            to_chain=to_chain,
            from_token=from_token,
            to_token=to_token,
            from_amount=from_amount,
            from_address=from_address
        )
        
        print(f"Quote received: {quote['tool']}")
        print(f"Expected output: {quote['estimate']['toAmount']}")
        print(f"Minimum output: {quote['estimate']['toAmountMin']}")
        
        # Transaction request is ready for signing
        print("\nTransaction request:")
        tx_request = quote["transactionRequest"]
        print(f"  To: {tx_request['to']}")
        print(f"  Value: {tx_request['value']}")
        print(f"  Gas Limit: {tx_request.get('gasLimit', 'auto')}")
        
        return quote
    
    
    def main():
        try:
            # Get available chains
            chains = get_chains()
            print(f"Found {len(chains)} chains")
            
            # Get quote for 10 USDC from Ethereum to Arbitrum
            quote = execute_transfer(
                from_chain=1,
                to_chain=42161,
                from_token="USDC",
                to_token="USDC",
                from_amount="10000000",  # 10 USDC (6 decimals)
                from_address="0x552008c0f6870c2f77e5cC1d2eb9bdff03e30Ea0"  # Replace
            )
            
            # After executing the transaction, poll for status:
            # result = poll_status(tx_hash, quote["tool"], 1, 42161)
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error: {e}")
    
    
    if __name__ == "__main__":
        main()

    export PRIVATE_KEY="0x..."

[​](https://docs.li.fi/agents/quick-start/code-samples#error-handling-patterns)

Error Handling Patterns
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both examples include these error handling patterns:

1.  **Exponential backoff** for rate limits (429)
2.  **Retry logic** for transient failures
3.  **Status polling** with timeout
4.  **Graceful error messages** for debugging

For more details on error handling, see [Error Playbooks](https://docs.li.fi/agents/reference/error-playbooks)
.

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

The apiKey allows you to authenticate on the API.

#### Body

application/json

Object describing what tokens to transfer and how to interact with the destination contracts.

Object defining instructions on how to perform multiple cross-chain/same-chain calls

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-from-chain)

fromChain

number

required

The sending chain. Can be the chain id or chain key

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-from-token)

fromToken

string

required

The token that should be transferred. Can be the address or the symbol

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-from-address)

fromAddress

string

required

The wallet that will send the transaction and contains the starting token

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-to-chain)

toChain

number

required

The receiving chain. Can be the chain id or chain key

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-to-token)

toToken

string

required

The token required to perform the contract interaction (can be something to stake, donate or to be used as payment)

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-to-amount)

toAmount

string

required

The amount of token required by the contract interaction. The LI.FI API will try and generate a quote that guarantees at least that amount on the destination chain.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-contract-calls)

contractCalls

Root Type for ContractCall · object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-to-fallback-address)

toFallbackAddress

string

If the call fails, use this address to send the bridged tokens to. If none is specified, the sending address will be used.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-contract-outputs-token)

contractOutputsToken

string

Some contract interactions will output a token. This is the case in things like staking. Omit this parameter if no token should be returned to the user.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-slippage)

slippage

number<double>

The maximum allowed slippage for the transaction as a decimal value. 0.005 represents 0.5%.

Required range: `0 <= x <= 1`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-integrator)

integrator

string

A string containing tracking information about the integrator of the API

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-referrer)

referrer

string

A string containing tracking information about the referrer of the integrator

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-allow-bridges)

allowBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that are allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-deny-bridges)

denyBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that are not allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-prefer-bridges)

preferBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that should be preferred for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-allow-exchanges)

allowExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that are allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-deny-exchanges)

denyExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that are not allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-prefer-exchanges)

preferExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that should be preferred for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-allow-destination-call)

allowDestinationCall

boolean

Whether swaps or other contract calls should be allowed as part of the destination transaction of a bridge transfer. Separate swap transactions on the destination chain are not affected by this flag. By default, parameter is `true`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#body-fee)

fee

number<double>

The percent of the integrator's fee that is taken from every transaction. The maximum fee amount should be less than 100%.

Required range: `0 <= x < 1`

#### Response

200 - application/json

Object listing all the currently enabled bridges and exchanges.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#response-exchanges)

exchanges

object\[\]

Show child attributes

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/perform-multiple-contract-calls-across-blockchains-beta#response-bridges)

bridges

object\[\]

Show child attributes

[Get a quote for a token transfer](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1)
[Get a set of routes for a request that describes a transfer of tokens](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/get-a-set-of-routes-for-a-request-that-describes-a-transfer-of-tokens)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# Stablecoin preset - LI.FI

[Skip to main content](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#content-area)

[LI.FI home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=f435348680e682acea6e3b9af339ed7a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=d02539147db168291d7c711beb45d10b)](https://docs.li.fi/)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

English

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

API presets

Stablecoin preset

[Overview](https://docs.li.fi/introduction/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction)
[JS/TS SDK](https://docs.li.fi/sdk/overview)
[Intent/Solver Marketplace](https://docs.li.fi/lifi-intents/introduction)
[Swap/Bridge Widget](https://docs.li.fi/widget/overview)
[Composer](https://docs.li.fi/composer/overview)
[Guides](https://docs.li.fi/guides/gas-subsidy)
[MCP Server](https://docs.li.fi/mcp-server/overview)
[For Agents](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview)
[FAQs](https://docs.li.fi/faqs/fees-monetization)

On this page

*   [Quick start](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#quick-start)
    
*   [Quote request (GET)](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#quote-request-get)
    
*   [Advanced routes (POST)](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#advanced-routes-post)
    
*   [JavaScript/TypeScript](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#javascript%2Ftypescript)
    
*   [Preset defaults](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#preset-defaults)
    
*   [Overrides example](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#overrides-example)
    
*   [Tool preferences](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#tool-preferences)
    
*   [Check supported stablecoins](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#check-supported-stablecoins)
    
*   [All stablecoins](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#all-stablecoins)
    
*   [Stablecoins on a specific chain](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#stablecoins-on-a-specific-chain)
    
*   [Related docs](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#related-docs)
    

Use the stablecoin preset when you need LI.FI to favor tight slippage and reliable routing for stablecoin moves. It is built for experiences such as:

*   Treasury and treasury-rebalance flows.
*   Larger cross-chain stablecoin transfers that demand predictable execution.
*   Integrations that require a safe default but still override specific fields when needed.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#quick-start)

Quick start
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Add `preset=stablecoin` to your quote or advanced routes request.
2.  Send the request as usual. LI.FI applies the preset defaults first, then merges any overrides you supply.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#quote-request-get)

Quote request (GET)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/quote?fromChain=1&toChain=137&fromToken=0xA0b86a33E6441b8C4C8C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C&toToken=0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174&fromAddress=0x123...&fromAmount=1000000000000000000&preset=stablecoin"
    

Review the full query parameter schema in the [`GET /v1/quote` reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#advanced-routes-post)

Advanced routes (POST)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST "https://li.quest/v1/advanced/routes" \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -d '{
        "fromChainId": 1,
        "toChainId": 137,
        "fromAmount": "1000000000000000000",
        "fromTokenAddress": "0xA0b86a33E6441b8C4C8C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C",
        "toTokenAddress": "0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174",
        "options": {
          "preset": "stablecoin"
        }
      }'
    

See the complete request body structure in the [`POST /v1/advanced/routes` reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/get-a-set-of-routes-for-a-request-that-describes-a-transfer-of-tokens)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#javascript/typescript)

JavaScript/TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    const quoteRequest = {
      fromChain: 1,
      toChain: 137,
      fromToken: "0xA0b86a33E6441b8C4C8C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C",
      toToken: "0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174",
      fromAddress: "0x123...",
      fromAmount: "1000000000000000000",
      preset: "stablecoin"
    };
    

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#preset-defaults)

Preset defaults
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The stablecoin preset configures these defaults to protect execution quality:

*   order: `CHEAPEST`
*   slippage: `0.001` (0.1%)
*   Price impact capped at 2%
*   Shortlist of bridges that are prime for stablecoin transfers
*   All exchanges enabled by default

If your request includes conflicting values, your request wins. For instance, when you supply `denyBridges` or similar list overrides, the preset’s defaults are replaced by the values you send. Include all bridges you want denied (existing and new) in the request payload.

This means you can override the preset defaults with your own values as shown below.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#overrides-example)

Overrides example
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    const routesRequestWithOverrides = {
      fromChainId: 1,
      toChainId: 137,
      fromAmount: "1000000000000000000",
      fromTokenAddress: "0xA0b86a33E6441b8C4C8C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C0C4C",
      toTokenAddress: "0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174",
      options: {
        preset: "stablecoin",
        slippage: 0.005, // loosen to 0.5% instead of the default 0.1%
        order: "FASTEST" // override the default CHEAPEST order
      }
    };
    

Integrators are advised to use the stablecoin preset as is and only override its values if absolutely necessary, since the default options are carefully optimized for stablecoin transfers.

To see all available options you can override, check the [options schema](https://github.com/lifinance/types/blob/main/src/api.ts#L116)
.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#tool-preferences)

Tool preferences
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For bridging, the preset prioritizes stablecoin-friendly paths such as:

*   Mint-and-burn flows like Glacis, Mayan Swift, Mayan MCTP, and Celer
*   Intent and solver-based options like Eco, Relay, Across, and Gaszip
*   Additional tools as they are vetted and added over time

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#check-supported-stablecoins)

Check supported stablecoins
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Stablecoin support is driven by LI.FI’s token tagging. Use [`/v1/tokens`](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens)
 with the `tags` filter to confirm which assets qualify.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#all-stablecoins)

All stablecoins

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/tokens?tags=stablecoin"
    

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#stablecoins-on-a-specific-chain)

Stablecoins on a specific chain

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://li.quest/v1/tokens?chains=ARB&tags=stablecoin"
    

Combine the `tags` filter with `chains` filters to match your integration. Need the full parameter list? Check the [`GET /v1/tokens` reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/fetch-all-known-tokens)
.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/presets/stablecoin#related-docs)

*   [`POST /v1/advanced/routes`](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/get-a-set-of-routes-for-a-request-that-describes-a-transfer-of-tokens)

Ask AI

      --url https://li.quest/v1/advanced/stepTransaction \

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#parameter-skip-simulation)

skipSimulation

boolean

Parameter to skip transaction simulation. The quote will be returned faster but the transaction gas limit won't be accurate.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#parameter-mayan-non-evm-permit-signature)

mayanNonEvmPermitSignature

boolean

Mayan specific option to bridge from non-EVM chain to Hyperliquid

#### Body

application/json

The step object

Object that represents one step of a `Route`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#body-id)

id

string

required

Unique identifier of the step

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#body-type)

type

enum<string>

required

The type of the step. `swap` executes a DEX swap on a single chain, `cross` bridges assets between chains, `lifi` runs LiFi's internal multi-action logic, and `protocol` represents protocol-level actions such as fee collection or vault interactions executed inside LiFi managed contracts.

Available options:

`swap`,

`cross`,

`lifi`,

`protocol`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#body-tool)

tool

string

required

The tool used for this step. E.g. `relay`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#body-action)

action

Root Type for Action · object

required

The action of the step

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "fromChainId": 100,  "fromAmount": "1000000000000000000",  "fromToken": {    "address": "0x63e62989d9eb2d37dfdb1f93a22f063635b07d51",    "symbol": "MIVA",    "decimals": 18,    "chainId": 100,    "name": "Minerva Wallet SuperToken",    "coinKey": "MIVA",    "priceUSD": "0.0455272371751059",    "logoURI": ""  },  "toChainId": 137,  "toToken": {    "address": "0xc0b2983a17573660053beeed6fdb1053107cf387",    "symbol": "MIVA",    "decimals": 18,    "chainId": 137,    "name": "Minerva Wallet SuperToken",    "coinKey": "MIVA",    "priceUSD": "0",    "logoURI": ""  },  "slippage": 0.003}

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#body-tool-details)

toolDetails

object

The details of the tool used for this step. E.g. `relay`

Show child attributes

transactionRequest

any

An ether.js TransactionRequest that can be triggered using a wallet provider. ([https://docs.ethers.io/v5/api/providers/types/#providers-TransactionRequest](https://docs.ethers.io/v5/api/providers/types/#providers-TransactionRequest)
)

200

application/json

Object that represents one step of a `Route`

id

string

required

Unique identifier of the step

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/advanced/populate-a-step-with-transaction-data#response-type)

type

enum<string>

required

The type of the step. `swap` executes a DEX swap on a single chain, `cross` bridges assets between chains, `lifi` runs LiFi's internal multi-action logic, and `protocol` represents protocol-level actions such as fee collection or vault interactions executed inside LiFi managed contracts.

Available options:

`swap`,

`cross`,

`lifi`,

`protocol`

tool

string

required

The tool used for this step. E.g. `relay`

Returns all possible connections based on a from- or toChain.

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://li.quest/v1/connections

200

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

string

The chain that should be the start of the possible connections.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-to-chain)

toChain

string

The chain that should be the end of the possible connections.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-from-token)

fromToken

string

Only return connections starting with this token.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-to-token)

toToken

string

Only return connections ending with this token.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-chain-types)

chainTypes

string

Restrict the resulting tokens to the given chainTypes.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-allow-bridges)

allowBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that are allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-deny-bridges)

denyBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that are not allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-prefer-bridges)

preferBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that should be preferred for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-allow-exchanges)

allowExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that are allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-deny-exchanges)

denyExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that are not allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-prefer-exchanges)

preferExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that should be preferred for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-allow-switch-chain)

allowSwitchChain

boolean

default:true

Whether connections that require chain switch should be included in the response.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#parameter-allow-destination-call)

allowDestinationCall

boolean

default:true

Whether connections that includes destination call should be included in the response.

#### Response

200 - application/json

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/returns-all-possible-connections-based-on-a-from-or-tochain#response-connections)

connections

Root Type for Connection · object\[\]

The possible connections

Show child attributes

[Get available bridges and exchanges](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-available-bridges-and-exchanges)
[Get gas price for the specified chainId](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/gas/get-gas-price-for-the-specified-chainid)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# Technical Requirements - LI.FI

[Skip to main content](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#content-area)

[LI.FI home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=f435348680e682acea6e3b9af339ed7a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=d02539147db168291d7c711beb45d10b)](https://docs.li.fi/)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

*   [Core Requirements](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#core-requirements)

*   [2\. Tokenised Position Return](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#2-tokenised-position-return)
    
*   [3\. Standard Deposit Function](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#3-standard-deposit-function)
    
*   [Deposit vs. Withdraw Support](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#deposit-vs-withdraw-support)
    
*   [After Integration](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#after-integration)
    
*   [Contact](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#contact)
    
*   [Related Pages](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#related-pages)
    

This page details the technical requirements your protocol must meet to be integrated with Composer.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#core-requirements)

Core Requirements
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#1-evm-compatibility)

1\. EVM Compatibility

Your protocol must be deployed on an **EVM-compatible chain**. Composer’s onchain VM executes compiled bytecode on EVM chains. Non-EVM chains (Solana, SUI, etc.) are not currently supported.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#2-tokenised-position-return)

2\. Tokenised Position Return

Upon deposit, your protocol must return a **token** to the user’s wallet. Composer routes are identified by the `toToken` parameter, which must be a valid ERC-20 token that represents the user’s position. **Supported token types:**

| Token Type | Example | Protocol Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ERC-4626 vault shares | Vault share tokens | Morpho, Euler |
| aTokens | Interest-bearing receipt tokens | Aave V3 |
| Liquid staking tokens | LSTs representing staked positions | Lido wstETH, EtherFi |
| Yield tokens | Tokens representing yield positions | Pendle, Ethena sUSDe |
| Custom receipt tokens | Protocol-specific deposit receipts | Felix Vanilla, Neverland |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#3-standard-deposit-function)

3\. Standard Deposit Function

Your deposit function should accept standard parameters that Composer’s eDSL compiler can encode. Common patterns include:

*   **ERC-4626 `deposit(uint256 assets, address receiver)`** — Standard vault interface
*   **Aave-style `supply(address asset, uint256 amount, address onBehalfOf, uint16 referralCode)`** — Lending pool interface
*   **Staking `stake(uint256 amount)`** or `wrap(uint256 amount)` — Staking/wrapping interface

Composer’s eDSL supports dynamic calldata injection, meaning the exact deposit amount is determined at execution time based on the output of preceding swap/bridge steps. Your deposit function must accept a standard amount parameter.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#deposit-vs-withdraw-support)

Deposit vs. Withdraw Support
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Composer supports two action types per protocol:

| Action | Description | Required? |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Deposit** | User sends tokens, receives position tokens | Yes (minimum) |
| **Withdraw** | User sends position tokens, receives underlying tokens | Optional |

Some protocols are integrated with **deposit only** (e.g., Kinetiq, Ethena, Maple). This is acceptable, and withdraw support can be added later.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#after-integration)

After Integration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once live, your protocol is accessible via:

Copy

Ask AI

    # Users can deposit from any token on any EVM chain
    curl -X GET 'https://li.quest/v1/quote?\
    fromChain=SOURCE_CHAIN_ID&\
    toChain=YOUR_PROTOCOL_CHAIN_ID&\
    fromToken=ANY_TOKEN_ADDRESS&\
    toToken=YOUR_VAULT_TOKEN_ADDRESS&\
    fromAddress=0xUSER_WALLET&\
    toAddress=0xUSER_WALLET&\
    fromAmount=AMOUNT'
    

LI.FI handles routing, bridging, swapping, and depositing automatically.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#contact)

Contact
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the integration process or ask questions, reach out to the LI.FI team:

*   **Email**: [support@li.fi](mailto:support@li.fi)
    
*   **Website**: [li.fi](https://li.fi/)
    

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements#related-pages)

# Integrate Your Protocol with Composer - LI.FI

[Skip to main content](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#content-area)

[LI.FI home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=f435348680e682acea6e3b9af339ed7a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/lifi/EmProAEgMrruLUbI/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=EmProAEgMrruLUbI&q=85&s=d02539147db168291d7c711beb45d10b)](https://docs.li.fi/)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

English

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

For Protocol Teams

Integrate Your Protocol with Composer

[Overview](https://docs.li.fi/introduction/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/introduction)

[For Agents](https://docs.li.fi/agents/overview)

On this page

*   [Why Integrate with Composer](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#why-integrate-with-composer)
    
*   [Reach Users on Every Chain](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#reach-users-on-every-chain)
    
*   [Distribution Through the LI.FI Ecosystem](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#distribution-through-the-li-fi-ecosystem)
    
*   [Better UX for Your Users](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#better-ux-for-your-users)
    
*   [Pre-Execution Simulation](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#pre-execution-simulation)
    
*   [Integration Requirements](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#integration-requirements)
    
*   [1\. EVM-Compatible Chain](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#1-evm-compatible-chain)
    
*   [2\. Tokenised Positions](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#2-tokenised-positions)
    
*   [3\. Standard Deposit Interface](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#3-standard-deposit-interface)
    
*   [Currently Integrated Protocols](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#currently-integrated-protocols)
    
*   [Getting Integrated](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#getting-integrated)
    
*   [What You Get](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#what-you-get)
    
*   [Next Steps](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#next-steps)
    

LI.FI Composer enables users to deposit into your protocol from **any token on any EVM chain** in a single transaction. This page explains why you should integrate and how the process works.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#why-integrate-with-composer)

Why Integrate with Composer
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#reach-users-on-every-chain)

Reach Users on Every Chain

Without Composer, users must manually bridge assets, swap tokens, and navigate to your protocol’s UI. With Composer, any user on any supported EVM chain can deposit into your protocol in one click, directly from wallets, dApps, and aggregators that integrate LI.FI.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#distribution-through-the-li-fi-ecosystem)

Distribution Through the LI.FI Ecosystem

LI.FI is integrated into hundreds of wallets, dApps, and DeFi platforms. When your protocol is available via Composer, it becomes accessible through:

*   **LI.FI API** — used by integrators building custom DeFi experiences
*   **LI.FI SDK** — TypeScript SDK for frontend and backend applications
*   **LI.FI Widget** — embeddable UI component used by wallets and dApps

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#better-ux-for-your-users)

Better UX for Your Users

Composer transforms multi-step, multi-chain operations into a single transaction:

| Without Composer | With Composer |
| --- | --- |
| Bridge assets to the right chain | One transaction |
| Swap to the required token | One signature |
| Approve the token | One click |
| Deposit into the protocol | Atomic execution |

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#pre-execution-simulation)

Pre-Execution Simulation

Every Composer transaction is simulated before execution, giving users certainty about the outcome before they sign. This reduces failed transactions and improves trust in your protocol.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#integration-requirements)

Integration Requirements
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To be integrated with Composer, your protocol must meet these requirements:

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#1-evm-compatible-chain)

1\. EVM-Compatible Chain

Composer currently supports **EVM-compatible chains only**. Solana and other non-EVM chains are not yet supported.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#2-tokenised-positions)

2\. Tokenised Positions

Your protocol must return a **tokenised position** to the user upon deposit. This includes:

*   **Vault tokens** (e.g., ERC-4626 vault shares)
*   **Receipt tokens** (e.g., Aave aTokens)
*   **Liquid staking tokens** (e.g., wstETH)
*   **Yield tokens** (e.g., Pendle yield tokens)

Protocols that do not return a token upon deposit are not currently supported.

### 

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#3-standard-deposit-interface)

3\. Standard Deposit Interface

Your protocol’s deposit function should follow standard patterns that Composer’s eDSL compiler can encode. The LI.FI team will work with you to ensure compatibility.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#currently-integrated-protocols)

Currently Integrated Protocols
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following protocols are already integrated with Composer, demonstrating the range of protocol types supported:

| Protocol | Type | Actions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Morpho V1 and V2 | Lending / Vaults | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Aave V3 | Lending | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Euler | Lending | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Lido wstETH | Liquid Staking | Deposit, Withdraw |
| EtherFi | Liquid Staking | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Pendle | Yield | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Felix Vanilla | Vaults | Deposit, Withdraw |
| HyperLend | Lending | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Neverland | Vaults | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Seamless | Lending | Deposit, Withdraw |
| USDai | Yield | Deposit, Withdraw |
| Kinetiq | Staking | Deposit |
| Kinetiq Earn (vkHYPE) | Yield | Deposit |
| Ethena | Yield | Deposit |
| Maple | Lending | Deposit |

For the full reference, see [Supported Protocols](https://docs.li.fi/composer/reference/supported-protocols)
.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#getting-integrated)

Getting Integrated
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrations are handled by the LI.FI team. Partner protocols can also be invited to contribute to the Composer backend codebase directly.[Apply for Composer Integration\
------------------------------\
\
Fill out the protocol integration form to start the process.](https://forms.gle/h1d265zuSWfQ3jsq9)
You can also reach out directly:

*   **GitHub**: [LI.FI GitHub](https://github.com/lifinance/)
    
*   **Email**: [marketing@li.finance](mailto:marketing@li.finance)
    

For detailed technical requirements, see [Technical Requirements](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/technical-requirements)
.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#what-you-get)

What You Get
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once integrated, your protocol is automatically available to:

*   **All LI.FI API integrators** — your vault/staking tokens appear as valid `toToken` destinations
*   **All LI.FI Widget deployments** — users can select your protocol’s tokens as destinations
*   **All LI.FI SDK users** — developers can build custom flows targeting your protocol

No additional work is required from your side after integration. LI.FI handles the routing, bridging, swapping, and deposit execution.

* * *

[​](https://docs.li.fi/composer/for-protocols/integration-guide#next-steps)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### Headers

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-x-lifi-api-key)

x-lifi-api-key

string

Authentication header, register in the LI.FI Partner Portal ([https://portal.li.fi/](https://portal.li.fi/)
 ) to get your API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-from-chain)

fromChain

string

required

The sending chain. Can be the chain id or chain key

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-to-chain)

toChain

string

required

The receiving chain. Can be the chain id or chain key

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-from-token)

fromToken

string

required

The token that should be transferred. Can be the address or the symbol

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-to-token)

toToken

string

required

The token that should be transferred to. Can be the address or the symbol

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-from-address)

fromAddress

string

required

The sending wallet address

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-to-address)

toAddress

string

The receiving wallet address. If none is provided, the fromAddress will be used

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-to-amount)

toAmount

string

required

The amount that will be received including all decimals (e.g. 1000000 for 1 USDC (6 decimals))

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-order)

order

enum<string>

Which kind of route should be preferred FASTEST: This sorting criterion prioritizes routes with the shortest estimated execution time. Users who value speed and want their transactions to be completed as quickly as possible should choose the fastest routes. CHEAPEST: This criterion focuses on minimizing the cost of the transaction, whether in token amount or USD amount (USD amount minus gas cost). Users looking for the most economical option should choose the cheapest routes.

Available options:

`FASTEST`,

`CHEAPEST`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-slippage)

slippage

number

The maximum allowed slippage for the transaction as a decimal value. 0.005 represents 0.5%.

Required range: `0 <= x <= 1`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-integrator)

integrator

string

A string containing tracking information about the integrator of the API

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-fee)

fee

number

The percent of the integrator's fee that is taken from every transaction. 0.02 represents 2%. The maximum fee amount should be less than 100%.

Required range: `0 <= x < 1`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-referrer)

referrer

string

A string containing tracking information about the referrer of the integrator

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-allow-bridges)

allowBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that are allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Also values `all`, `none`, `default` and `[]` are acceptable and mean all tools of the current type (`all`), no tools (for `none` and `[]` cases) and default tool's settings on the current stage.

Bridge tool identifier or keyword. Retrieve current bridge keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Supported keywords: `all`, `none`, `default`, `[]`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-allow-exchanges)

allowExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that are allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Also values `all`, `none`, `default` and `[]` are acceptable and mean all tools of the current type (`all`), no tools (for `none` and `[]` cases) and default tool's settings on the current stage.

Exchange tool identifier or keyword. Retrieve current exchange keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Supported keywords: `all`, `none`, `default`, `[]`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-deny-bridges)

denyBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that are not allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Also values `all`, `none`, `default` and `[]` are acceptable and mean all tools of the current type (`all`), no tools (for `none` and `[]` cases) and default tool's settings on the current stage.

Bridge tool identifier or keyword. Retrieve current bridge keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Supported keywords: `all`, `none`, `default`, `[]`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-deny-exchanges)

denyExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that are not allowed for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Also values `all`, `none`, `default` and `[]` are acceptable and mean all tools of the current type (`all`), no tools (for `none` and `[]` cases) and default tool's settings on the current stage.

Exchange tool identifier or keyword. Retrieve current exchange keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Supported keywords: `all`, `none`, `default`, `[]`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-prefer-bridges)

preferBridges

string\[\]

List of bridges that should be preferred for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Also values `all`, `none`, `default` and `[]` are acceptable and mean all tools of the current type (`all`), no tools (for `none` and `[]` cases) and default tool's settings on the current stage.

Bridge tool identifier or keyword. Retrieve current bridge keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Supported keywords: `all`, `none`, `default`, `[]`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-prefer-exchanges)

preferExchanges

string\[\]

List of exchanges that should be preferred for this transaction. Retrieve the current catalog from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Also values `all`, `none`, `default` and `[]` are acceptable and mean all tools of the current type (`all`), no tools (for `none` and `[]` cases) and default tool's settings on the current stage.

Exchange tool identifier or keyword. Retrieve current exchange keys from the `/v1/tools` endpoint. Supported keywords: `all`, `none`, `default`, `[]`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-allow-destination-call)

allowDestinationCall

boolean

Whether swaps or other contract calls should be allowed as part of the destination transaction of a bridge transfer. Separate swap transactions on the destination chain are not affected by this flag. By default, parameter is `true`.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-max-price-impact)

maxPriceImpact

number

The price impact threshold above which routes are hidden. As an example, one should specify 0.15 (15%) to hide routes with more than 15% price impact. The default is 10%.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-swap-step-timing-strategies)

swapStepTimingStrategies

string\[\]

Timing setting to wait for a certain amount of swap rates. In the format `minWaitTime-${minWaitTimeMs}-${startingExpectedResults}-${reduceEveryMs}`. Please check [docs.li.fi](https://docs.li.fi/)
 for more details.

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#parameter-route-timing-strategies)

routeTimingStrategies

string\[\]

Timing setting to wait for a certain amount of routes to be generated before chosing the best one. In the format `minWaitTime-${minWaitTimeMs}-${startingExpectedResults}-${reduceEveryMs}`. Please check [docs.li.fi](https://docs.li.fi/)
 for more details.

#### Response

200

application/json

The step populated with the transaction data

Object that represents one step of a `Route`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#response-id)

id

string

required

Unique identifier of the step

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#response-type)

type

enum<string>

required

The type of the step. `swap` executes a DEX swap on a single chain, `cross` bridges assets between chains, `lifi` runs LiFi's internal multi-action logic, and `protocol` represents protocol-level actions such as fee collection or vault interactions executed inside LiFi managed contracts.

Available options:

`swap`,

`cross`,

`lifi`,

`protocol`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#response-tool)

tool

string

required

The tool used for this step. E.g. `relay`

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#response-action)

action

Root Type for Action · object

required

The action of the step

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "fromChainId": 100,  "fromAmount": "1000000000000000000",  "fromToken": {    "address": "0x63e62989d9eb2d37dfdb1f93a22f063635b07d51",    "symbol": "MIVA",    "decimals": 18,    "chainId": 100,    "name": "Minerva Wallet SuperToken",    "coinKey": "MIVA",    "priceUSD": "0.0455272371751059",    "logoURI": ""  },  "toChainId": 137,  "toToken": {    "address": "0xc0b2983a17573660053beeed6fdb1053107cf387",    "symbol": "MIVA",    "decimals": 18,    "chainId": 137,    "name": "Minerva Wallet SuperToken",    "coinKey": "MIVA",    "priceUSD": "0",    "logoURI": ""  },  "slippage": 0.003}

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#response-tool-details)

toolDetails

object

The details of the tool used for this step. E.g. `relay`

Show child attributes

[​](https://docs.li.fi/api-reference/get-a-quote-for-a-token-transfer-1#response-estimate)

estimate

The estimation for the step
